<h4 data-start="580" data-end="624" class="">2. <strong data-start="588" data-end="624">Layout polu√≠do e pouco intuitivo</strong></h4>

<h4 data-start="885" data-end="924" class="">3. <strong data-start="893" data-end="924">Falta de valida√ß√£o de dados</strong></h4>

streamlit_code = <span class="hljs-string">"""
import streamlit as st
from PIL import Image
import pytesseract
import fitz  # PyMuPDF
import pandas as pd
import io

st.set_page_config(page_title="OCR Extractor", layout="centered")
st.title("üìÑ Extra√ß√£o de Texto de PDF, Imagem ou Planilha")

st.markdown("Fa√ßa upload de um arquivo PDF, imagem (PNG, JPG) ou planilha Excel. O sistema extrair√° o conte√∫do automaticamente.")

uploaded_file = st.file_uploader("Selecione o arquivo", type=["pdf", "png", "jpg", "jpeg", "xlsx"])

def extract_text_from_pdf(file):
    text = ""
    with fitz.open(stream=file.read(), filetype="pdf") as doc:
        for page in doc:
            text += page.get_text()
    return text

def ocr_from_image(file):
    image = Image.open(file)
    text = pytesseract.image_to_string(image)
    return text

def extract_from_excel(file):
    df = pd.read_excel(file)
    return df

    file_type

<h3 data-start="771" data-end="816" class="">‚úÖ 3. Envie os arquivos para o reposit√≥rio</h3>

<h3 data-start="1144" data-end="1187" class="">üíª <strong data-start="1151" data-end="1187">B. M√©todo via Git (mais t√©cnico)</strong></h3>
